Gradient stencils based on lattice Boltzmann stencils. 

Isotropic gradient stencil based on D2\+Q9 lattice Boltzmann stencil. It is the same as the 8 point 2D Gradient stencil from "{}\+M.\+Alfaraj, Y. Wang and Y. Luo, Geophysical prospecting 62 (2014) 507-\/517"{}
